## <a name="windows-server-2008"></a><span data-ttu-id="e2db4-443">Windows Server 2008</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e2db4-443">Windows Server 2008</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="e2db4-444">屬性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e2db4-444">Attributes</span></span>](#windows-server-2008-attributes)

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="e2db4-1574">備註</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e2db4-1574">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e2db4-1575">**MS DFSR 內容** 類別是分散式檔案系統 (DFS) Replication service 支援的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e2db4-1575">The **ms-DFSR-Content** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
